msg:I have lived in many five-star hotels for so many years. No matter what problems I encounter, I seldom make bad reviews, because it is not easy, but this time I must tell what happened. I live in Zhuanghe, often When I went to Dandong, I booked a parent-child room on Ctrip. The price was a little expensive. It was 788 yuan with three breakfasts. The child was only two years old. Breakfast was also free. The total is to stay with the child and go out for a stroll. It takes an hour and 10 minutes to drive to the hotel , Checked in at 3:30 in the afternoon. When I entered the hotel, I found that many people were checking in. It should be a team situation, but there was only one person at the front desk of the hotel. I was dizzy and had to wait. I waited for about 20 minutes before checking in. The front desk They said that they have to pay 1,500 yuan for the room fee and deposit. I feel that I have stayed in a five-star hotel that requires the most deposit. After entering the room, I found that there are a lot less entertainment facilities for children in the room, and Ctrip said before that the size of the house 50 square meters, but it feels like 35 square meters at most. Tell yourself that since you have already checked in, donâ€™t think so much. Ask the front desk why the entertainment facilities in the room are different from the photos on Ctrip? Some wines can be made up after receiving feedback, and some have not been purchased because of collective purchases. I was speechless ğŸ˜“, and then I found the main problem. I booked a parent-child room, which is the room with the best price in the hotel except for the presidential suite. The key The room window is not a river view room! I could only see the very limited area of the Yalu River from the window, and I felt bad for a moment. I told myself, it doesnâ€™t matter, donâ€™t think too much, and then drove my wife and children to the city for dinner. After dinner, I returned to the hotel. At 8 o'clock in the evening, my family called to tell me that there was an urgent matter at home, and I had to rush back to Zhuanghe tonight, so I contacted the hotel front desk as soon as possible to explain the reason for checking out. I would like to make a special explanation here. The reason for this is mine, itâ€™s my own reason, part of the room fee can be deducted, and it doesnâ€™t matter how much the room fee is refunded, because I think the hotel should not deduct all the room fee, after all, there are still three breakfasts that we havenâ€™t eaten yet. No matter what, the breakfast money should be refunded to us, but the answer is that it has been 4 and a half hours since check-in, and the room fee cannot be refunded! At that time, I felt very angry, because I was the reason for this incident, and I had to rush back to my hometown overnight because of an urgent matter at home. Even if the three breakfasts were refunded to me, it was unreasonable for the hotel not to refund a penny. The management staff said it was too late, and the room was sold that day, and the time I checked in was not the peak tourist season, and there are probably a lot of vacant rooms in the hotel, well, I will accept the full deduction of the room fee, but you At least I should have returned the three breakfasts to me. At the time, I should have left straight away because of the rush. When I left, the hotel staff on duty expressed embarrassment and said they understood me very well, but thatâ€™s what the hotel management staff said. After communicating with Ctrip and the hotel, the feedback he got was that the hotel The cleaning staff has already left work, and there is no staff to re-clean the room. Let me explain that from check-in to check-out, I have not touched any furnishings in the room. Such a large hotel has tried every means to find various reasons for this room fee. I was also drunk, and the communication was fruitless. The day after tomorrow, Ctrip also very much agreed with my statement, and unilaterally refunded 200 yuan to me. Here, I am very grateful to Ctrip. What I care about is not how much the room fee is refunded, but what I care about. It is the attitude of the hotel in dealing with the problem.
